Dukapaṭṭhāna

[page 001]
                                                                                 1
           Namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammāsambuddhassa.
                         [I. DUKA-PAṬṬHĀNAṂ.
                               I.
                          HETU-DUKAṂ.]

                          [Anulomaṃ.]
     1. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ1 paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho; adosaṃ paṭicca alobho
amoho; amohaṃ paṭicca alobho adoso. Lobhaṃ paṭicca
moho; mohaṃ paṭicca lobho; dosaṃ paṭicca moho; mohaṃ
paṭicca doso.2 Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe3 . . .
     2. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā citta-
samuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     3. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā
uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca khandhā
cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ4)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 So R. and K. B. and S. hetudhammaṃ always.
2 None of the texts collated give lobho and doso as
     mutually conditioned.
3 None of the texts collated give the excisions in this
     con- nexion. R. has nowhere . . . pe . . .
4 See above under 1. Only K. has bandhitabbaṃ.


[page 002]
2                          Hetudukaṃ.
. . . Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho sampayuttakā ca khandhā
cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhik-
khaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā cittasam-
uṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.1 Paṭisandhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca
vatthu,2 vatthuṃ paṭicca khandhā; ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . .
pe . . .3
     5. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati
hetupaccayā.
     Nahetū khandhe paṭicca hetū. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe
vatthuṃ paṭicca hetū.
     6. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā
uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā hetū ca
cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve khandhe paṭicca dve
khandhā hetu ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭi-
sandhikkhaṇe vatthuṃ paṭicca hetū ca sampayuttakā ca
khandhā.
     7. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo
uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Alobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca adoso
amoho . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobhañ ca sam-
payuttake ca khandhe paṭicca moho, dosañ ca sampayuttake
ca khandhe paṭicca moho. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe alobhañ ca
vatthuñ ca paṭicca adoso amoho . . . pe . . .
     8. Hetuñ ca na hetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu
dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā
cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Dve khandhe ca hetuñ ca
paṭicca dve khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Paṭi-
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 R. adds, Dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā
     cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ.
2 S. and K. usually read vatthuṃ. B. and R. vatthu.
     B. vatthu also in accusative.
3 All texts excise. To be read presumably with tayo . . .
     dve . . . dve. Cf. pp. 6, 7, § 4 with khandhā in this §.


[page 003]
                          Anekapaccayā.                3
sandhikkhaṇe vatthuñ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca sampayuttakā
khandhā.
     9. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu
ca dhammā uppajjanti hetupaccayā.
     Nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca alobhañ ca paṭicca tayo
khandhā adoso amoho cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve
khandhe ca alobhañ ca paṭicca dve khandhā adoso amoho
cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . .
nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca lobhañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā
moho ca cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ . . . pe . . . dve
khandhe . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe vatthuñ ca alo-
bhañ ca paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca khandhā
. . . pe . . .
     Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati āram-
maṇapaccayā . . . (rūpaṃ chaḍḍetvā arūpe yeva nava
pañhā)1 . . . adhipatipaccayā . . . (paṭisandhi natthi, pari-
puṇṇaṃ). Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ paṭicca . . . pe . . . mahā-
bhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ, upādā rūpaṃ (idaṃ
ninnānaṃ)2 . . .
anantarapaccayā . . .
samanantarapaccayā . . .
sahajātapaccayā . . . (sabbe mahābhūtā yāva asaññasattā) . . .
aññamaññapaccayā . . .
nissayapaccayā . . .
upanissayapaccayā3 . . .
purejātapaccayā4 . . .
āsevanapaccayā . . . (dvīsu5 paṭisandhi natthi) . . .
kammapaccayā . . .
vipākapaccayā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . .
avigatapaccayā . . .
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 S. ārammaṇapaccayā rūpaṃ. Chaḍḍetvā arūpe ye ca neva neva pañhā.
     B. paccayā rūpaṃ chaḍḍetvā || arūpe ca nava pañhā.
2 S. Adhipatipaccayā paṭisandhi natthi paripuṇṇaṃ. Naṃ mahābhūtaṃ
     paṭicca. Mahābhūte paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānan rūpaṃ idanānaṃ.
     B. Idaṃ nānaṃ. R. imaṃ nānaṃ.
3 S. omits.
4 B. pūre- always.
5 R. dvīsu pi.


[page 004]
4                          Hetudukaṃ.
          Hetuyā nava,                     sabbattha nava,
          ārammaṇe nava,                    avigate nava:--
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                          Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.
                          [Paccaniyaṃ.]
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
nahetupaccayā.
     Ahetukaṃ nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā
cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .1 Ahetukapaṭisan-
dhikkhaṇe khandhe paṭicca vatthu, vatthuṃ paṭicca
khandhā. Ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . . bāhiraṃ āhāra-
samuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ2 . . . pe . . .
     5. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetudhammo uppajjati
nahetupaccayā.
     Vicikicchāsahagate uddhaccasahagate khandhe paṭicca
vicikicchāsahagato uddhaccasahagato moho.
     2. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
nārammaṇapaccayā.
     Hetuṃ paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhik-
khaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
nārammaṇapaccayā.
     Nahetū khandhe3 paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . (sabbe mahābhūtā) . . .
     8. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu
dhammo uppajjati nārammaṇapaccayā.
     Hetuñ ca nahetū ca khandhe paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ
rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
nādhipatipaccayā4 . . . (paripuṇṇaṃ) . . . nānantarapaccayā5
. . . nasamanantarapaccayā . . . na aññamaññapaccayā
. . . na upanissayapaccayā . . .
     1. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati
napurejātapaccayā.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 Cf. p. 2, 6.
2 B. āhāraṃ utuṃ asañña (sic). R. āhāra || utu || asañña ||.
     S. āhāraṃ utu.
3 S. nahetu khandhaṃ.
4 R. na-adhi-.
5 R. na-anant-.


[page 005]
                Napurejātapaccayavāro. Arūpaṃ.     5
     Arūpe alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho . . . (cakkaṃ
bandhitabbaṃ)1 . . . Lobhaṃ paṭicca moho, mohaṃ paṭicca
lobho . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     2. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe hetuṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā. Hetuṃ
paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . .
pe . . .
     3. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā
uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe alobhaṃ paṭicca adoso amoho sampayuttakā ca
khandhā . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Lobhaṃ paṭicca
moho sampayuttakā ca khandhā . . . pe2 . . . Paṭisan-
dhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā.
Dve khandhe paṭicca dve khandhā.3 Nahetū khandhe paṭicca
cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     5. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati
napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe nahetū khandhe paṭicca hetū. Paṭisandhikkhaṇe
. . . pe . . .
     6. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca nahetu ca dhammā
uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo khandhā hetū
ca; dve khandhe . . . pe . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     7. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo
uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe alobhañ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca adoso
amoho, . . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . arūpe lobhañ ca
sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca moho . . . (cakkaṃ
bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     8. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu
dhammo uppajjati napurejātapaccayā.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 Cf. p. 1 under 1. S. adds dhammaṃ.
2 B. and R. repeat cakkaṃ.
3 R. omits sentence.


[page 006]
6                          Hetudukaṃ.
     Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca hetuñ ca paṭicca tayo
khandhā . . . pe . . . dve khandhe . . . pe . . . nahetū
khandhe ca hetuñ ca paṭicca cittasamuṭṭhānaṃ rūpaṃ.
Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     9. Hetuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu ca
nahetu ca dhammā uppajjanti napurejātapaccayā.
     Arūpe nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ ca alobhaṃ ca paṭicca tayo
khandhā adoso amoho ca; . . . pe . . . dve khandhe
. . . (cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ) . . . nahetuṃ ekaṃ khandhañ
ca lobhañ ca paṭicca tayo khandhā moho ca; . . . (cakkaṃ
bandhitabbaṃ) . . . Paṭisandhikkhaṇe . . . pe . . .
     1. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati
napacchājātapaccayā: . . . pe . . . nāsevanapaccayā1
. . . pe . . .
     2. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
nakammapaccayā.
     Hetuṃ paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā.
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
nakammapaccayā.
     Nahetū khandhe paṭicca sampayuttakā cetanā. Bāhi-
raṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ.
     8. Heṭuñ ca nahetuñ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu
dhammo uppajjati nakammapaccayā.
     Hetuñ ca sampayuttake ca khandhe paṭicca sampayuttakā
cetanā.
     1. Hetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca hetu dhammo uppajjati
navipākapaccayā: . . . pe . . .2
     4. Nahetuṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca nahetu dhammo uppajjati
nāhārapaccayā.
     Bāhiraṃ utusamuṭṭhānaṃ3 asaññasattānaṃ. Ekaṃ mahā-
--------------------------------------------------------------------------

2 R. adds (nava).
3 B. utuṃ asañña || na jhānapaccayā || bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ utuṃ asañña
     sattānaṃ mahābhūte paṭicca rūpajīvitindriyaṃ || najhānapaccayā ||
     pañcaviññāṇaṃ bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ utuṃ asañña namaggapaccayā ||
     S. utu . . . asañña . . . na indriyapacca . . . bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ
     utu . . . asañña indriyapacca bāhiraṃ āhāraṃ utu . . .
     asaññasattānaṃ, etc.

bhūtaṃ paṭicca tayo mahābhūtā. Mahābhūte paṭicca
kaṭattā-rūpaṃ upādā-rūpaṃ . . . pe . . .1
. . . na indriyapaccayā . . . Bāhiraṃ āhārasamuṭṭhānaṃ

          Nahetuyā dve,                     nakamme tīṇi,
          nārammaṇe tīṇi,                navipāke nava,
          nādhipatiyā nava,6                nāhāre ekaṃ,
          nānantare tīṇi,6                na-indriye10 ekaṃ,
          nasamanantare7 tīṇi,           najhāne ekaṃ,
          na-aññamaññe8 tīṇi,               namagge ekaṃ,
          na-upanissaye tīṇi,               nasampayutte tīṇi,
          napurejāte nava,                navippayutte nava,
          napacchājāte9 nava,               nonatthiyā tīṇi,
          nāsevane nava.6                novigate tīṇi:--
evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.

          napacchājāte nava,3

          Nahetupaccayā,4 ārammaṇe          indriye dve,
          dve,                          jhāne dve,
          anantare dve (saṃkhittaṃ),      magge ekaṃ,

                     Paccaniyānulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.5

abhinandati, taṃ garuṃ katvā rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi

thuñ ca tiṇṇannaṃ . . . pe . . .
     8. Nahetu-sahetuko ca . . . nahetu-ahetukassa . . .
     Sahajātaṃ, pacchājātaṃ āhāraṃ indriyaṃ. Sahajātā
nahetu-sahetukā khandhā ca mahābhūtā ca cittasamuṭṭhā-
nānaṃ rūpānaṃ atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā
nahetu-sahetukā khandhā ca kabaḷiṃkāro āhāro ca imassa
kāyassa atthipaccayena paccayo. Pacchājātā nahetu-sahe-
tukā khandhā ca rūpajīvitindriyañ ca kaṭattā rūpānaṃ
atthipaccayena paccayo.
          Ārammaṇe cattāri,                vipāke cattāri,
          adhipatiyā cattāri,               āhāre cattāri,
          anantare cattāri,                indriye cattāri,
          samanantare cattāri,           jhāne cattāri,
          sahajāte satta,                magge tīṇi,
          aññamaññe cha,                    sampayutte dve,
          nissaye satta,                    vippayutte tīṇi,
          upanissaye cattāri,               atthiyā satta,
          purejāte dve,                     natthiyā cattāri,
          pacchājāte dve,                vigate cattāri,
          āsevane dve,                     avigate satta:--
          kamme cattāri,
     evaṃ gaṇetabbaṃ.
                               Anulomaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ.

     Dānaṃ sīlaṃ uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati,
pubbe suciṇṇāni paccavekkhati, jhānā vuṭṭhahitvā jhānaṃ

vekkhanti, phalaṃ paccavekkhanti.1 Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa

     Ārammaṇādhipati:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . kabaḷiṃkāraṃ

rāgo uppajjati diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa . . .
     Ārammaṇādhipati, sahajātādhipati. Ārammaṇādhipati:--
dānaṃ . . . (saṃkhittaṃ) . . . nibbānaṃ maggassa phalassa
adhipatipaccayena paccayo. Arūpino khandhe garuṃ katvā
assādeti . . . rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi uppajjati. Sahajātādhi-
pāti:-- arūpī adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ adhi-
patipaccayena paccayo.
     5. Arūpī dhammo rūpissa dhammassa adhipatipaccayena
paccayo.
     Sahajātādhipati:-- arūpī adhipati cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ
rūpānaṃ adhipatipaccayena paccayo.
     6. Arūpī dhammo rūpissa . . . ca arūpissa . . .
     Sahajātādhipati:-- arūpī adhipati sampayuttakānaṃ
khandhānaṃ cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ adhipatipacca-
yena paccayo.
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa anantarapacca-
yena paccayo.
     Purimā purimā arūpino khandhā pacchimānaṃ pacchi-
mānaṃ arūpīnaṃ1 khandhānaṃ phalasamāpattiyā anantara-
paccayena paccayo . . . samanantarapaccayena paccayo
. . . sahajātapaccayena paccayo . . . (satta, miha
ghaṭanā2 natthi) . . . aññamaññapaccayena paccayo . . .
nissayapaccayena paccayo . . . (satta pañhā, miha ghaṭanā2
natthi).
     2. Rūpī dhammo arūpissa upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇūpanissayo pakatūpanissayo . . . pe . . . Paka-
tūpanissayo:-- utu3 bhojanaṃ senāsanaṃ upanissāya dānaṃ
deti . . . pe . . . saṃghaṃ bhindati. Utu3 bhojanaṃ senā-
sanaṃ saddhāya . . . pe4 . . . phalasamāpattiyā upanissaya-
paccayena paccayo.

                               Kammavāro.                         129
     4. Arūpī dhammo arūpissa dhammassa upannissayapac-

     Ārammaṇūpanissayo . . .1pe . . . Pakatūpanissayo:--

pe . . . phalasamāpattiyā upanissayapaccayena paccayo.
     2. Rūpī dhammo arūpissa2 dhammassa purejātapacca-
yena paccayo.
     Ārammaṇapurejātaṃ, vatthupurejātaṃ. Ārammaṇapure-
jātaṃ:-- cakkhuṃ . . . pe . . . vatthuṃ kabaḷiṃkāraṃ āhāraṃ
aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppajjati; dibbena cakkhunā
rūpaṃ passati, dibbāya sotadhātuyā saddaṃ suṇāti; rūpā-

     1. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavasampayuttassa dham-

     2. Āsavasampayutto dhammo āsavavippayuttassa . . .
     Sahajātā, nānākhaṇikā. Sahajātā āsavasampayuttā cetanā
cittasamuṭṭhānānaṃ rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
Nānākhaṇikā āsavasampayuttā cetanā vipākānaṃ khandhā-
naṃ kaṭattā ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo. Doman-
assa-, vicikicchā-, uddhacca-sahagatā cetanā mohassa citta-
samuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ kammapaccayena paccayo.
     3. Āsavasampayutto . . . āsavasampayuttassa ca . . .

yuttakānaṃ khandhānaṃ mohassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ

                     ĀSAVO-CEVA-SĀSAVA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Āsavañ ceva sāsavañ ca dhammaṃ1 paṭicca āsavo ceva
sāsavo ca dhammo2 uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Kāmāsavaṃ paṭicca3 diṭṭhāsavo avijjāsavo . . . (cakkaṃ
bandhitabbaṃ). Bhavāsavaṃ paṭicca4 avijjāsavo . . .
(cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ). Diṭṭhāsavaṃ paṭicca avijjāsavo.
     2. Āsavañ ceva sāsavañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca sāsavo ceva
no ca āsavo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Āsave5 paṭicca sampayuttakā khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ
ca rūpaṃ.
     3. Āsavañ ceva sāsavañ ca dhammaṃ paṭicca āsavo ceva
sāsavo ca sāsavo ceva no ca āsavo ca dhammā6 uppajjanti
hetupaccayā.
     Kāmāsavaṃ paṭicca diṭṭhāsavo avijjāsavo sampayuttakā
khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ. Bhavāsavaṃ . . .
(cakkaṃ bandhitabbaṃ).
     4. Sāsavaṃ ceva no ca āsavaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca sāsavo
ceva no ca āsavo dhammo uppajjati hetupaccayā.
     Sāsavaṃ ceva no ca āsavaṃ ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca tayo
khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . . Paṭisan-

khandhā; ekaṃ mahābhūtaṃ . . . pe . . .

                          [XXX.
                GANTHO-CEVA-GANTHASAMPAYUTTA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Ganthañ ceva ganthasampayuttaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca

     Sīlabbataparāmāsakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca abhijjhākāya-

sakāyagantho; idaṃsaccābhinivesakāyaganthaṃ paṭicca

saccābhinivesakāyagantho.

ganthasampayutto ceva no ca gantho dhammo . . .

diṭṭhi uppajjati. Diṭṭhiṃ assādeti . . . rāgo diṭṭhi uppajjati.
     2. Parāmāsasampayutto . . . parāmāsavippayuttassa . . .
     Ariyā parāmāsasampayutte pahībakilese paccavekkhanti,
vikkhambhitakilese paccavekkhanti, pubbe samudāciṇṇe
kilese jānanti, parāmāsasampayutte khandhe aniccato vipas-
santi . . . assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha parāmāsa-
vippayutto rāgo, diṭṭhi,3 vicikicchā, uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ
uppajjati. Cetopariyañāṇena parāmāsasampayuttacitta-
samaṃgissa cittaṃ jānāti. Parāmāsasampayuttā khandhā
cetopariyañāṇassa pubbenivāsānussatiñāṇassa yathākam-
mūpagañāṇassa anāgataṃsañāṇassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇa-
paccayena paccayo.
     4. Parāmāsavippayutto . . . parāmāsavippayuttassa . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati,
assādeti . . .4 uppajjati. Pubbe suciṇṇāni . . . jhānā
. . . Ariyā maggā vuṭṭhahitvā maggaṃ paccavekkhanti,
phalaṃ, nibbānaṃ paccavekkhanti. Nibbānaṃ gotrabhussa
yodānassa maggassa phalassa āvajjanāya ārammaṇapacca-
yena paccayo. Ariyā parāmāsavippayutte pahīnakilese
vikkhambhitakilese . . . pubbe . . . cakkhuṃ . . .

     6. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāsassa ca . . .
     Parāmaṭṭhā ceva no ca parāmāsā hetū sampayuttakānaṃ
khandhānaṃ parāmāsassa ca cittasamuṭṭhānānañ ca rūpānaṃ
hetupaccayena paccayo.
     1. Parāmāso ceva parāmaṭṭho ca . . . dhammassa āram-
maṇapaccayena paccayo . . . (tīṇi ārabbha1 kātabbāni;
parāmāsdukasadisaṃ).
     4. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso . . .
     Dānaṃ, sīlaṃ, uposathakammaṃ katvā taṃ paccavekkhati,
assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo uppajjati, diṭṭhi,2
vicikicchā, uddhaccaṃ, domanassaṃ uppajjati. Pubbe . . .
jhānā . . . Ariyā . . . gotrabhuṃ paccavekkhanti, vodānaṃ
paccavekkhanti, pahīnakilese, vikkhambhitakilese . . . pubbe
. . . cakkhuṃ . . . vatthuṃ parāmaṭṭhe ceva no ca parā-
māse khandhe aniccato . . . pe . . . domanassaṃ uppaj-
jati. Dibbena cakkhunā rūpaṃ passati . . . (yāva āvaj-
janā3 sabbaṃ kātabbaṃ).
     5. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca parāmāso dhammo parāmā-
sassa ceva parāmaṭṭhassa dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena
paccayo.
     Dānaṃ . . .4 Pubbe . . . jhānā . . . cakkhuṃ . . . khandhe
assādeti, abhinandati, taṃ ārabbha rāgo1 uppajjati1 diṭṭhi
. . . pe . . .
     6. Parāmaṭṭho ceva no ca . . . parāmāsassa ceva parā-
maṭṭhassa ca parāmaṭṭhassa ceva no ca parāmasassa ca
dhammassa ārammaṇapaccayena paccayo.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 Cf. p. 9. K. kātabbā.
2 R. omits.
3 K. āvajjanāya. Cf. p. 1O.
4 As under 4.


[page 352]
352                Parāmāso-ceva-parāmaṭṭhadukaṃ.
     Dānaṃ, silaṃ, uposathakammaṃ . . . pubbe . . . jhānā
cakkhuṃ . . .1 aniccato vipassati, assādeti abhinandati, taṃ
ārabbha parāmāso ca sampayuttakā ca khandhā uppajjanti.
(Evaṃ itare pi tīṇi ārabbha kātabbāni.2 Imaṃ dukaṃ parā-
māsadukasadisaṃ. Lokuttaraṃ yamhi na labbhati, tamhi na
kātabbaṃ.3)
               PARĀMĀSO-CEVA-PARĀMAṬṬHA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.

1 As under 4.
2 K. and B. -bā.
3 R. yamhiṃ . . . tamhiṃ.
     B. has only lokuttaraṃ bāhīraṃ (sic) kātabbaṃ.

                          [XLIII.
           PARĀMĀSAVIPPAYUTTA-PARĀMAṬṬHA-DUKAṂ.]
     1. Parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭhaṃ dhammaṃ paṭicca
parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭho dhammo uppajjati hetu-
paccayā.
     Parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭhaṃ1 ekaṃ khandhaṃ paṭicca
tayo khandhā cittasamuṭṭhānañ ca rūpaṃ; dve . . .
     4. Parāmāsavippayutta-aparāmaṭṭhaṃ2 dhammaṃ paṭicca
parāmāsavippayutta-aparāmaṭṭho dhammo uppajjati hetu-
paccayā . . . (saṃkhittaṃ; yathā cūḷantaraduke lokiyadukaṃ
evaṃ kātabbaṃ. Ninnānākaraṇaṃ).
           PARĀMĀSAVIPPAYUTTA-PARĀMAṬṬHA-DUKAṂ niṭṭhitaṃ.
--------------------------------------------------------------------------
1 R. -yuttaṃ parā-.
2 K. repeats formula 1.
     K. NOTE. Ito paraṃ Parāmāso-ceva-parāmāsasampa-
     yutta-dukassa vibhaṃgo amhākaṃ potthake pi. Sīhaḷapot-
     thake pi na dissati. Parāmāsaduka-parāmāso ceva-parā-
     maṭṭhaduka-parāmāsavippayuttaparāmaṭṭhadukāni pi Sīha-
     ḷapotthake na paññāyanti. Etāni amhākaṃ potthake. Pāḷina-
     yānusāren' eva sodhitāni.
